# Text Elements
L,
| alignment seq | ^05WGWMjd

cytochrome P450 of Clostridium ...,
    "RGKMPNT...Q" ^AWdk7eUw

# a.a.
"types"
= 21

one-hot ^WZj4SqRo

# seqs
align columns ^2xocJYFy

K ^N7z1QgHm

1 ^nawLm0UY

flatten ^2bQBYni4

MSA seq length = ~600 seqs, assume trim to 10%
21 amino acids
> 845 000 seqs in MSA, assume prune to ~5%

60 x 21 x (~0.05 x 845 000)
    = 53 235 000
/\ well, one-hot so 53 235 000/21 = 2 535 000 ^0duKLfjf

latent
m dims

^ m arbitrary ^0WDMU2Mn

initialize to ^ULB48R88

prior
p(z) ^59eRuvLq

H_dec ^jFf94NQV

soft
max ^z1he4Wmi
